  807. # [06:17] <vlad> hg qimport -r <your-patch-revision>
  808. # [06:17] <vlad> hg qpop
  809. # [06:17] <vlad> hg pull -u
  810. # [06:17] <vlad> hg qpush
  811. # [06:17] <nrc> hg strip is my magic sauce for fixing everything, but I don't really know how to use it - every time I try from the command line it gets messed up. But using Tortoise Hg with strip can usually fix anything I manage to screw up. Sorry that's not very usefuyl
  812. # [06:17] <vlad> basically, take your imported-patch-rev and turn it into a mq patch, then pop it
  813. # [06:18] <vlad> "hg strip" just deletes the specified commits.. you could do "hg strip <your patch revision>" as well, and then pull -u, and re-import it
  814. # [06:19] <spohl> vlad: I did 'hg import' in order to do an 'hg push', not an 'hg qimport' for a 'hg qpush'...
  815. # [06:19] <spohl> vlad: but between 'hg import' and 'hg push' I slipped up and did 'hg pull'
  816. # [06:20] <vlad> spohl: sure, so after you qpush, 'hg qrm -r qtip' and it'll become a regular commit instead of a mq one
  817. # [06:20] * Joins: elin (elin@moz-99690620.hinet-ip.hinet.net)

  821. # [06:22] <@gavin> spohl: hg strip 'roots(outgoing())'
